[09:37:47.982]                     else if (inherits(cond, "warning")) {
[09:37:47.982]                       muffled <- grepl(pattern, "muffleWarning")
[09:37:47.982]                       if (muffled)

[09:37:47.982]                         for (restart in restarts) {

[09:37:47.982]                             next

[09:37:47.982]                           break

[09:37:47.982]                     invisible(muffled)
